</p></div><div class="_2wEhX" id="1-1-seoContent"><h3 class="type-sm color-ui-black font-bold" data-test-id="panelHeading">With us, you know you’re getting the best</h3><p class="type-sm color-ui-black" data-test-id="panelCopy"><p>In the last five years we've invested nearly $145 billion to improve everything from voice and streaming quality to data downloads and call reliability. So when our performance was put to the test across the U.S., Puerto Rico and the U.S. Virgin Islands, it was no surprise that AT&amp;T was named the <span class=""><a aria-label="nation's best network" class="_20CgK _1QRfu" href="/offers/network.html" rel="noopener">nation's best network</a></span>.* And now we're continuing to innovate by building the next generation of wireless technology: <span class=""><a aria-label="5G" class="_20CgK _1QRfu" href="/5g/consumer/" rel="noopener">5G</a></span>. Join us and see what's next.</p>
</p></div><div class="_2wEhX" id="1-2-seoContent"><h3 class="type-sm color-ui-black font-bold" data-test-id="panelHeading">Move without the stress</h3><p class="type-sm color-ui-black" data-test-id="panelCopy"><p>Whether you’re a longtime customer or a potential new prospect, <span class=""><a aria-label="moving with AT&amp;T" class="_20CgK _1QRfu" href="https://www.att.com/moving/" rel="noopener">moving with AT&amp;T</a></span> is easy. <span class=""><a aria-label="Find the perfect package" class="_20CgK _1QRfu" href="https://www.att.com/moving/new-customers.html" rel="noopener">Find the perfect package</a></span> for your new home or follow a few easy steps to  <span class=""><a aria-label="transfer your current services" class="_20CgK _1QRfu" href="https://www.att.com/shop/move/existing.html" rel="noopener">transfer your current services</a></span>. Enjoy your favorite entertainment while you unpack with <span class=""><a aria-label="DIRECTV" class="_20CgK _1QRfu" href="https://www.att.com/directv/" rel="noopener">DIRECTV</a></span> and <span class=""><a aria-label="AT&amp;T Internet" class="_20CgK _1QRfu" href="https://www.att.com/internet/" rel="noopener">AT&amp;T Internet</a></span>.</p>
</p></div></div></div><div class="row"><div class="grid-col-12"><div class="_3Eehw _VIAiH"><span>*Best network claim based on GWS OneScore Sept. 2018. </span></div></div></div></div></div><section
